1e:T41f40,<h1 id="skills-galaxy-from-concept-to-implementation" class="group relative text-4xl font-bold mt-8 mb-4 text-foreground leading-tight">
            <a href="#skills-galaxy-from-concept-to-implementation" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Skills Galaxy: From Concept to Implementation">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Skills Galaxy: From Concept to Implementation
        </h1>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">Imagine if your skills could orbit around you like planets in a solar system, rotating in an orderly and beautiful manner around you as the “sun” - what kind of visual experience would that be? …Well, I won’t force the metaphor anymore. In summary, I wanted to showcase key but ordinary information through a creative form, breaking away from the so-called “boring list layout” to give people a sense of “Wow! That’s interesting!”</p>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">Through the tech stack of React, TypeScript, Framer Motion, and native requestAnimationFrame, we can create such high-performance animation effects.</p>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">Next, I will start from the most fundamental mathematical principles and gradually dive deep into every implementation detail, comprehensively analyzing the implementation principles of the Skills Galaxy.</p>
<h2 id="mathematical-foundation-of-circular-motion" class="group relative text-3xl font-semibold mt-6 mb-3 text-foreground leading-tight">
            <a href="#mathematical-foundation-of-circular-motion" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Mathematical Foundation of Circular Motion">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Mathematical Foundation of Circular Motion
        </h2>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">Everything begins with mathematics. To make planets rotate around a center, we first need to understand how to convert rotation angles into specific coordinate positions on the screen.</p>
<h3 id="polar-coordinate-system-conversion" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#polar-coordinate-system-conversion" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Polar Coordinate System Conversion">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Polar Coordinate System Conversion
        </h3>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">In our galaxy, each planet follows the rules of a polar coordinate system. Polar coordinates use <code>(r, θ)</code> to describe a point’s position - <code>r</code> is the distance to the center (orbital radius), and <code>θ</code> is the angle. This description method is perfect for circular motion because we only need to change the angle to make planets move along circular orbits.</p>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">But the browser world uses a Cartesian coordinate system, using <code>(x, y)</code> to position elements. So we need coordinate conversion:</p>

            <div class="enhanced-codeblock relative mb-6 rounded-lg border bg-background border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden shadow-sm" data-enhanced-codeblock="true" data-language="typescript" data-code="%2F%2F%20This%20is%20the%20core%20formula%20that%20makes%20planets%20%22spin%22%0Aconst%20planetX%20%3D%20galaxyCenter.x%20%2B%20Math.cos(angle%20*%20Math.PI%20%2F%20180)%20*%20orbitRadius%3B%0Aconst%20planetY%20%3D%20galaxyCenter.y%20%2B%20Math.sin(angle%20*%20Math.PI%20%2F%20180)%20*%20orbitRadius%3B">
                <div class="codeblock-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-surface border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700">
                    <span class="codeblock-language text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide text-foreground opacity-70 inline">typescript</span>
                    <button class="codeblock-copy-btn inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 text-xs font-medium border rounded transition-all duration-200 bg-background hover:bg-surface text-foreground hover:text-primary border-gray-300 dark:border-gray-600 hover:scale-105 active:scale-95" title="Copy code">
                        <svg class="copy-icon w-4 h-4" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path d="M8 3a1 1 0 011-1h2a1 1 0 110 2H9a1 1 0 01-1-1z" />
                            <path d="M6 3a2 2 0 00-2 2v11a2 2 0 002 2h8a2 2 0 002-2V5a2 2 0 00-2-2 3 3 0 01-3 3H9a3 3 0 01-3-3z" />
                        </svg>
                        <svg class="copied-icon w-4 h-4 hidden" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.707 5.293a1 1 0 010 1.414l-8 8a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 011.414-1.414L8 12.586l7.293-7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        <span class="copy-text inline">Copy</span>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <pre class="codeblock-content p-4 overflow-x-auto font-mono text-sm leading-relaxed bg-surface text-foreground"><code class="language-typescript"><span class="hljs-comment inline">// This is the core formula that makes planets &quot;spin&quot;</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> planetX = galaxyCenter.<span class="hljs-property inline">x</span> + <span class="hljs-title class_ inline">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">cos</span>(angle * <span class="hljs-title class_ inline">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-property inline">PI</span> / <span class="hljs-number inline">180</span>) * orbitRadius;
<span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> planetY = galaxyCenter.<span class="hljs-property inline">y</span> + <span class="hljs-title class_ inline">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">sin</span>(angle * <span class="hljs-title class_ inline">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-property inline">PI</span> / <span class="hljs-number inline">180</span>) * orbitRadius;
</code></pre>
            </div>
        
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">There are several key points worth noting:</p>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>galaxyCenter.x</code> and <code>galaxyCenter.y</code> are the center coordinates of the galaxy</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>Math.cos()</code> and <code>Math.sin()</code> are trigonometric functions responsible for converting angles to coordinates</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>angle * Math.PI / 180</code> converts the angle from degrees to radians (JavaScript’s trigonometric functions require radians)</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>orbitRadius</code> is the orbital radius, determining how far the planet is from the center</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="simple-example-making-a-point-rotate" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#simple-example-making-a-point-rotate" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Simple Example: Making a Point Rotate">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Simple Example: Making a Point Rotate
        </h3>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">Let me use the simplest example to demonstrate this principle:</p>

            <div class="enhanced-codeblock relative mb-6 rounded-lg border bg-background border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden shadow-sm" data-enhanced-codeblock="true" data-language="typescript" data-code="%2F%2F%20Assume%20we%20have%20a%20center%20point%20(400%2C%20300)%20and%20a%20circle%20with%20radius%20100px%0Aconst%20centerX%20%3D%20400%3B%0Aconst%20centerY%20%3D%20300%3B%0Aconst%20radius%20%3D%20100%3B%0Alet%20angle%20%3D%200%3B%0A%2F%2F%20Update%20position%20every%20frame%0Afunction%20updatePosition()%20%7B%0Aconst%20x%20%3D%20centerX%20%2B%20Math.cos(angle%20*%20Math.PI%20%2F%20180)%20*%20radius%3B%0Aconst%20y%20%3D%20centerY%20%2B%20Math.sin(angle%20*%20Math.PI%20%2F%20180)%20*%20radius%3B%0A%2F%2F%20Update%20element%20position%0Aelement.style.left%20%3D%20x%20%2B%20'px'%3B%0Aelement.style.top%20%3D%20y%20%2B%20'px'%3B%0A%2F%2F%20Increment%20angle%20to%20make%20it%20rotate%0Aangle%20%2B%3D%201%3B%0ArequestAnimationFrame(updatePosition)%3B%0A%7D">
                <div class="codeblock-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-surface border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700">
                    <span class="codeblock-language text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide text-foreground opacity-70 inline">typescript</span>
                    <button class="codeblock-copy-btn inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 text-xs font-medium border rounded transition-all duration-200 bg-background hover:bg-surface text-foreground hover:text-primary border-gray-300 dark:border-gray-600 hover:scale-105 active:scale-95" title="Copy code">
                        <svg class="copy-icon w-4 h-4" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path d="M8 3a1 1 0 011-1h2a1 1 0 110 2H9a1 1 0 01-1-1z" />
                            <path d="M6 3a2 2 0 00-2 2v11a2 2 0 002 2h8a2 2 0 002-2V5a2 2 0 00-2-2 3 3 0 01-3 3H9a3 3 0 01-3-3z" />
                        </svg>
                        <svg class="copied-icon w-4 h-4 hidden" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.707 5.293a1 1 0 010 1.414l-8 8a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 011.414-1.414L8 12.586l7.293-7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        <span class="copy-text inline">Copy</span>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <pre class="codeblock-content p-4 overflow-x-auto font-mono text-sm leading-relaxed bg-surface text-foreground"><code class="language-typescript"><span class="hljs-comment inline">// Assume we have a center point (400, 300) and a circle with radius 100px</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> centerX = <span class="hljs-number inline">400</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> centerY = <span class="hljs-number inline">300</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> radius = <span class="hljs-number inline">100</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword inline">let</span> angle = <span class="hljs-number inline">0</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment inline">// Update position every frame</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword inline">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_ inline">updatePosition</span>(<span class="hljs-params inline"></span>) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> x = centerX + <span class="hljs-title class_ inline">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">cos</span>(angle * <span class="hljs-title class_ inline">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-property inline">PI</span> / <span class="hljs-number inline">180</span>) * radius;
    <span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> y = centerY + <span class="hljs-title class_ inline">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">sin</span>(angle * <span class="hljs-title class_ inline">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-property inline">PI</span> / <span class="hljs-number inline">180</span>) * radius;
    
    <span class="hljs-comment inline">// Update element position</span>
    element.<span class="hljs-property inline">style</span>.<span class="hljs-property inline">left</span> = x + <span class="hljs-string inline">&#x27;px&#x27;</span>;
    element.<span class="hljs-property inline">style</span>.<span class="hljs-property inline">top</span> = y + <span class="hljs-string inline">&#x27;px&#x27;</span>;
    
    <span class="hljs-comment inline">// Increment angle to make it rotate</span>
    angle += <span class="hljs-number inline">1</span>;
    
    <span class="hljs-title function_ inline">requestAnimationFrame</span>(updatePosition);
}
</code></pre>
            </div>
        
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">This is the foundation of circular motion - the Skills Galaxy’s rotation effect is built upon this basic principle.</p>
<h2 id="multi-orbit-system-implementation-strategy" class="group relative text-3xl font-semibold mt-6 mb-3 text-foreground leading-tight">
            <a href="#multi-orbit-system-implementation-strategy" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Multi-Orbit System Implementation Strategy">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Multi-Orbit System Implementation Strategy
        </h2>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">Now we know how to make one planet rotate, but a real galaxy needs multiple orbits, needs to reasonably distribute planets, and needs to make them look natural without being crowded.</p>
<h3 id="how-is-the-number-of-orbits-specified-and-how-are-planets-evenly-distributed-among-these-orbits" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#how-is-the-number-of-orbits-specified-and-how-are-planets-evenly-distributed-among-these-orbits" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to How is the number of orbits specified? And how are planets evenly distributed among these orbits?">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            How is the number of orbits specified? And how are planets evenly distributed among these orbits?
        </h3>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">We actually specify an upper limit for the number of orbits, which is determined by the number of skills:</p>

            <div class="enhanced-codeblock relative mb-6 rounded-lg border bg-background border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden shadow-sm" data-enhanced-codeblock="true" data-language="typescript" data-code="const%20orbitIndex%20%3D%20index%20%25%207%3B">
                <div class="codeblock-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-surface border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700">
                    <span class="codeblock-language text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide text-foreground opacity-70 inline">typescript</span>
                    <button class="codeblock-copy-btn inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 text-xs font-medium border rounded transition-all duration-200 bg-background hover:bg-surface text-foreground hover:text-primary border-gray-300 dark:border-gray-600 hover:scale-105 active:scale-95" title="Copy code">
                        <svg class="copy-icon w-4 h-4" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path d="M8 3a1 1 0 011-1h2a1 1 0 110 2H9a1 1 0 01-1-1z" />
                            <path d="M6 3a2 2 0 00-2 2v11a2 2 0 002 2h8a2 2 0 002-2V5a2 2 0 00-2-2 3 3 0 01-3 3H9a3 3 0 01-3-3z" />
                        </svg>
                        <svg class="copied-icon w-4 h-4 hidden" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.707 5.293a1 1 0 010 1.414l-8 8a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 011.414-1.414L8 12.586l7.293-7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        <span class="copy-text inline">Copy</span>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <pre class="codeblock-content p-4 overflow-x-auto font-mono text-sm leading-relaxed bg-surface text-foreground"><code class="language-typescript"><span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> orbitIndex = index % <span class="hljs-number inline">7</span>;
</code></pre>
            </div>
        
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">Here, this upper limit is 7, meaning there are at most 7 orbits.</p>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">For example, if we have 15 skills:</p>

            <div class="enhanced-codeblock relative mb-6 rounded-lg border bg-background border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden shadow-sm" data-enhanced-codeblock="true" data-language="" data-code="Skill%200%3A%20index%3D0%2C%20orbitIndex%3D0%257%3D0%20%E2%86%92%201st%20orbit%0ASkill%201%3A%20index%3D1%2C%20orbitIndex%3D1%257%3D1%20%E2%86%92%202nd%20orbit%0ASkill%202%3A%20index%3D2%2C%20orbitIndex%3D2%257%3D2%20%E2%86%92%203rd%20orbit%0A...%0ASkill%207%3A%20index%3D7%2C%20orbitIndex%3D7%257%3D0%20%E2%86%92%20Back%20to%201st%20orbit%0ASkill%208%3A%20index%3D8%2C%20orbitIndex%3D8%257%3D1%20%E2%86%92%202nd%20orbit">
                <div class="codeblock-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-surface border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700">
                    <span class="codeblock-language text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide text-foreground opacity-70 inline">code</span>
                    <button class="codeblock-copy-btn inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 text-xs font-medium border rounded transition-all duration-200 bg-background hover:bg-surface text-foreground hover:text-primary border-gray-300 dark:border-gray-600 hover:scale-105 active:scale-95" title="Copy code">
                        <svg class="copy-icon w-4 h-4" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path d="M8 3a1 1 0 011-1h2a1 1 0 110 2H9a1 1 0 01-1-1z" />
                            <path d="M6 3a2 2 0 00-2 2v11a2 2 0 002 2h8a2 2 0 002-2V5a2 2 0 00-2-2 3 3 0 01-3 3H9a3 3 0 01-3-3z" />
                        </svg>
                        <svg class="copied-icon w-4 h-4 hidden" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.707 5.293a1 1 0 010 1.414l-8 8a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 011.414-1.414L8 12.586l7.293-7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        <span class="copy-text inline">Copy</span>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <pre class="codeblock-content p-4 overflow-x-auto font-mono text-sm leading-relaxed bg-surface text-foreground"><code>Skill 0: <span class="hljs-attribute inline">index</span>=0, <span class="hljs-attribute inline">orbitIndex</span>=0%7=0 → 1st orbit
Skill 1: <span class="hljs-attribute inline">index</span>=1, <span class="hljs-attribute inline">orbitIndex</span>=1%7=1 → 2nd orbit
Skill 2: <span class="hljs-attribute inline">index</span>=2, <span class="hljs-attribute inline">orbitIndex</span>=2%7=2 → 3rd orbit
<span class="hljs-built_in inline">..</span>.
Skill 7: <span class="hljs-attribute inline">index</span>=7, <span class="hljs-attribute inline">orbitIndex</span>=7%7=0 → Back <span class="hljs-keyword inline">to</span> 1st orbit
Skill 8: <span class="hljs-attribute inline">index</span>=8, <span class="hljs-attribute inline">orbitIndex</span>=8%7=1 → 2nd orbit
</code></pre>
            </div>
        
<h3 id="orbital-radius-calculation" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#orbital-radius-calculation" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Orbital Radius Calculation">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Orbital Radius Calculation
        </h3>

            <div class="enhanced-codeblock relative mb-6 rounded-lg border bg-background border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden shadow-sm" data-enhanced-codeblock="true" data-language="typescript" data-code="const%20orbitRadius%20%3D%20100%20%2B%20orbitIndex%20*%2050%3B%20%2F%2F%20100px%2C%20150px%2C%20200px%2C%20250px%2C%20300px%2C%20350px%2C%20400px%20orbits">
                <div class="codeblock-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-surface border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700">
                    <span class="codeblock-language text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide text-foreground opacity-70 inline">typescript</span>
                    <button class="codeblock-copy-btn inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 text-xs font-medium border rounded transition-all duration-200 bg-background hover:bg-surface text-foreground hover:text-primary border-gray-300 dark:border-gray-600 hover:scale-105 active:scale-95" title="Copy code">
                        <svg class="copy-icon w-4 h-4" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path d="M8 3a1 1 0 011-1h2a1 1 0 110 2H9a1 1 0 01-1-1z" />
                            <path d="M6 3a2 2 0 00-2 2v11a2 2 0 002 2h8a2 2 0 002-2V5a2 2 0 00-2-2 3 3 0 01-3 3H9a3 3 0 01-3-3z" />
                        </svg>
                        <svg class="copied-icon w-4 h-4 hidden" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.707 5.293a1 1 0 010 1.414l-8 8a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 011.414-1.414L8 12.586l7.293-7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        <span class="copy-text inline">Copy</span>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <pre class="codeblock-content p-4 overflow-x-auto font-mono text-sm leading-relaxed bg-surface text-foreground"><code class="language-typescript"><span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> orbitRadius = <span class="hljs-number inline">100</span> + orbitIndex * <span class="hljs-number inline">50</span>; <span class="hljs-comment inline">// 100px, 150px, 200px, 250px, 300px, 350px, 400px orbits</span>
</code></pre>
            </div>
        
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">The radius of each orbit increases according to the pattern <code>100 + orbitIndex * 50</code>:</p>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed">1st orbit: 100px</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed">2nd orbit: 150px</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed">3rd orbit: 200px</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed">…and so on up to 400px</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="preventing-planets-from-clustering-together-at-the-start" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#preventing-planets-from-clustering-together-at-the-start" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Preventing planets from clustering together at the start">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Preventing planets from clustering together at the start
        </h3>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">To prevent planets from overlapping on the same orbit initially, I assigned different initial angles to each planet:</p>

            <div class="enhanced-codeblock relative mb-6 rounded-lg border bg-background border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden shadow-sm" data-enhanced-codeblock="true" data-language="typescript" data-code="const%20%5Bangle%2C%20setAngle%5D%20%3D%20useState(index%20*%2060)%3B%20%2F%2F%20Initial%20angle%20increases%20by%20index">
                <div class="codeblock-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-surface border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700">
                    <span class="codeblock-language text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide text-foreground opacity-70 inline">typescript</span>
                    <button class="codeblock-copy-btn inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 text-xs font-medium border rounded transition-all duration-200 bg-background hover:bg-surface text-foreground hover:text-primary border-gray-300 dark:border-gray-600 hover:scale-105 active:scale-95" title="Copy code">
                        <svg class="copy-icon w-4 h-4" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path d="M8 3a1 1 0 011-1h2a1 1 0 110 2H9a1 1 0 01-1-1z" />
                            <path d="M6 3a2 2 0 00-2 2v11a2 2 0 002 2h8a2 2 0 002-2V5a2 2 0 00-2-2 3 3 0 01-3 3H9a3 3 0 01-3-3z" />
                        </svg>
                        <svg class="copied-icon w-4 h-4 hidden" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.707 5.293a1 1 0 010 1.414l-8 8a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 011.414-1.414L8 12.586l7.293-7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        <span class="copy-text inline">Copy</span>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <pre class="codeblock-content p-4 overflow-x-auto font-mono text-sm leading-relaxed bg-surface text-foreground"><code class="language-typescript"><span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> [angle, setAngle] = <span class="hljs-title function_ inline">useState</span>(index * <span class="hljs-number inline">60</span>); <span class="hljs-comment inline">// Initial angle increases by index</span>
</code></pre>
            </div>
        
<h3 id="visual-implementation-of-orbits" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#visual-implementation-of-orbits" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Visual Implementation of Orbits">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Visual Implementation of Orbits
        </h3>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">The orbits themselves are created through CSS as transparent circular rings:</p>

            <div class="enhanced-codeblock relative mb-6 rounded-lg border bg-background border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden shadow-sm" data-enhanced-codeblock="true" data-language="html" data-code="div%0AclassName%3D%22absolute%20border%20border-white%2F10%20rounded-full%20pointer-events-none%22%0Astyle%3D%7B%7B%0Awidth%3A%20orbitRadius%20*%202%2C%0Aheight%3A%20orbitRadius%20*%202%2C%0Aleft%3A%20galaxyCenter.x%20-%20orbitRadius%2C%0Atop%3A%20galaxyCenter.y%20-%20orbitRadius%2C%0A%7D%7D%0A%2F%3E">
                <div class="codeblock-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-surface border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700">
                    <span class="codeblock-language text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide text-foreground opacity-70 inline">html</span>
                    <button class="codeblock-copy-btn inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 text-xs font-medium border rounded transition-all duration-200 bg-background hover:bg-surface text-foreground hover:text-primary border-gray-300 dark:border-gray-600 hover:scale-105 active:scale-95" title="Copy code">
                        <svg class="copy-icon w-4 h-4" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path d="M8 3a1 1 0 011-1h2a1 1 0 110 2H9a1 1 0 01-1-1z" />
                            <path d="M6 3a2 2 0 00-2 2v11a2 2 0 002 2h8a2 2 0 002-2V5a2 2 0 00-2-2 3 3 0 01-3 3H9a3 3 0 01-3-3z" />
                        </svg>
                        <svg class="copied-icon w-4 h-4 hidden" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.707 5.293a1 1 0 010 1.414l-8 8a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 011.414-1.414L8 12.586l7.293-7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        <span class="copy-text inline">Copy</span>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <pre class="codeblock-content p-4 overflow-x-auto font-mono text-sm leading-relaxed bg-surface text-foreground"><code class="language-html"><span class="hljs-tag inline">&lt;<span class="hljs-name inline">div</span>
    <span class="hljs-attr inline">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string inline">&quot;absolute border border-white/10 rounded-full pointer-events-none&quot;</span>
    <span class="hljs-attr inline">style</span>=<span class="hljs-string inline">{{</span>
        <span class="hljs-attr inline">width:</span> <span class="hljs-attr inline">orbitRadius</span> * <span class="hljs-attr inline">2</span>,
        <span class="hljs-attr inline">height:</span> <span class="hljs-attr inline">orbitRadius</span> * <span class="hljs-attr inline">2</span>,
        <span class="hljs-attr inline">left:</span> <span class="hljs-attr inline">galaxyCenter.x</span> <span class="hljs-attr inline">-</span> <span class="hljs-attr inline">orbitRadius</span>,
        <span class="hljs-attr inline">top:</span> <span class="hljs-attr inline">galaxyCenter.y</span> <span class="hljs-attr inline">-</span> <span class="hljs-attr inline">orbitRadius</span>,
    }}
/&gt;</span>
</code></pre>
            </div>
        
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">There’s an important detail here: <code>left: galaxyCenter.x - orbitRadius</code>. Because CSS positioning is based on the element’s top-left corner, we need to offset left and up by one orbital radius distance to align the circle’s center with the galaxy center.</p>
<h2 id="z-index-and-rendering-layer-control" class="group relative text-3xl font-semibold mt-6 mb-3 text-foreground leading-tight">
            <a href="#z-index-and-rendering-layer-control" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Z-index and Rendering Layer Control">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Z-index and Rendering Layer Control
        </h2>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">In a 3D effect that requires hierarchical relationships, managing the layering between elements is crucial. Here’s how it works:</p>

            <div class="enhanced-codeblock relative mb-6 rounded-lg border bg-background border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden shadow-sm" data-enhanced-codeblock="true" data-language="typescript" data-code="%2F%2F%20Sun%20center%20-%20highest%20layer%0Adiv%20className%3D%22absolute%20z-20%20w-24%20h-24%20...%22%3E%0A%2F%2F%20Orbits%20-%20no%20mouse%20event%20response%0A%2F%2F%20Planets%20-%20interactive%20layer">
                <div class="codeblock-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-surface border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700">
                    <span class="codeblock-language text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide text-foreground opacity-70 inline">typescript</span>
                    <button class="codeblock-copy-btn inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 text-xs font-medium border rounded transition-all duration-200 bg-background hover:bg-surface text-foreground hover:text-primary border-gray-300 dark:border-gray-600 hover:scale-105 active:scale-95" title="Copy code">
                        <svg class="copy-icon w-4 h-4" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path d="M8 3a1 1 0 011-1h2a1 1 0 110 2H9a1 1 0 01-1-1z" />
                            <path d="M6 3a2 2 0 00-2 2v11a2 2 0 002 2h8a2 2 0 002-2V5a2 2 0 00-2-2 3 3 0 01-3 3H9a3 3 0 01-3-3z" />
                        </svg>
                        <svg class="copied-icon w-4 h-4 hidden" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.707 5.293a1 1 0 010 1.414l-8 8a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 011.414-1.414L8 12.586l7.293-7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        <span class="copy-text inline">Copy</span>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <pre class="codeblock-content p-4 overflow-x-auto font-mono text-sm leading-relaxed bg-surface text-foreground"><code class="language-typescript"><span class="hljs-comment inline">// Sun center - highest layer</span>
&lt;motion.<span class="hljs-property inline">div</span> className=<span class="hljs-string inline">&quot;absolute z-20 w-24 h-24 ...&quot;</span>&gt;

<span class="hljs-comment inline">// Orbits - no mouse event response</span>
&lt;div className=&quot;... pointer-events-none&quot;&gt;

// Planets - interactive layer
&lt;motion.div className=&quot;... pointer-events-auto&quot;&gt;
</code></pre>
            </div>
        
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">This design has several key points:</p>
<ol class="list-decimal list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Sun always in front</strong>: <code>z-20</code> ensures the central sun won’t be obscured by planets</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Orbits don’t interfere with interaction</strong>: <code>pointer-events-none</code> allows users to click planets on the orbit, not the orbit itself</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Planets can interact</strong>: <code>pointer-events-auto</code> makes each planet responsive to mouse events</li>
</ol>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">This layering design allows users to naturally interact with planets while maintaining clear visual hierarchy.</p>
<h2 id="animation-loop-implementation" class="group relative text-3xl font-semibold mt-6 mb-3 text-foreground leading-tight">
            <a href="#animation-loop-implementation" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Animation Loop Implementation">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Animation Loop Implementation
        </h2>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">Now we come to the most crucial part - how to make this galaxy smoothly rotate.</p>
<h3 id="why-choose-requestanimationframe" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#why-choose-requestanimationframe" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Why choose requestAnimationFrame?">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Why choose requestAnimationFrame?
        </h3>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">Compared to <code>setInterval</code> or <code>setTimeout</code>, <code>requestAnimationFrame</code> has several irreplaceable advantages:</p>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Synchronized with browser refresh rate</strong>: Usually 60fps, giving users the smoothest experience</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Automatic optimization</strong>: Pauses when the page is not visible, saving CPU resources</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Time precision</strong>: Provides high-precision timestamps</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="core-animation-loop-implementation" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#core-animation-loop-implementation" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Core Animation Loop Implementation">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Core Animation Loop Implementation
        </h3>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">Here’s the core code for achieving smooth animation:</p>

            <div class="enhanced-codeblock relative mb-6 rounded-lg border bg-background border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden shadow-sm" data-enhanced-codeblock="true" data-language="typescript" data-code="const%20animate%20%3D%20(currentTime%3A%20number)%20%3D%3E%20%7B%0Aif%20(!lastTimeRef.current)%20lastTimeRef.current%20%3D%20currentTime%3B%0Aconst%20deltaTime%20%3D%20currentTime%20-%20lastTimeRef.current%3B%0AlastTimeRef.current%20%3D%20currentTime%3B%0AframeCountRef.current%2B%2B%3B%0A%2F%2F%20Frame%20rate%20control%20strategy%20-%20update%20position%20every%202%20frames%0Aif%20(frameCountRef.current%20%25%202%20%3D%3D%3D%200)%20%7B%0Aconst%20currentData%20%3D%20planetsDataRef.current%3B%0A%2F%2F%20Update%20planet%20positions%20and%20angles%0Aconst%20updatedPlanets%20%3D%20currentData.map(planet%20%3D%3E%20%7B%0Aif%20(planet.isPaused)%20return%20planet%3B%0Aconst%20baseSpeed%20%3D%200.15%20%2B%20planet.orbitIndex%20*%200.08%3B%0Aconst%20currentSpeed%20%3D%20baseSpeed%20*%20planet.speedMultiplier%20*%20planet.collisionSpeedBoost%3B%0Aconst%20newAngle%20%3D%20(planet.angle%20%2B%20currentSpeed%20*%20deltaTime%20*%200.01)%20%25%20360%3B%0Aconst%20normalizedAngle%20%3D%20newAngle%200%20%3F%20newAngle%20%2B%20360%20%3A%20newAngle%3B%0Areturn%20%7B%0A...planet%2C%0Aangle%3A%20normalizedAngle%2C%0Ax%3A%20galaxyCenter.x%20%2B%20Math.cos(normalizedAngle%20*%20Math.PI%20%2F%20180)%20*%20planet.orbitRadius%2C%0Ay%3A%20galaxyCenter.y%20%2B%20Math.sin(normalizedAngle%20*%20Math.PI%20%2F%20180)%20*%20planet.orbitRadius%2C%0A%7D%3B%0A%7D)%3B%0A%2F%2F%20Collision%20detection%20every%204%20frames%20(maintain%20high%20frequency%20during%20stirring)%0Alet%20finalPlanets%20%3D%20updatedPlanets%3B%0Aif%20(frameCountRef.current%20%25%204%20%3D%3D%3D%200%20%7C%7C%20isStirring)%20%7B%0AfinalPlanets%20%3D%20detectCollisions(updatedPlanets)%3B%0A%7D%0A%2F%2F%20Only%20update%20state%20when%20there%20are%20actual%20changes%0Aif%20(finalPlanets%20!%3D%3D%20currentData)%20%7B%0AplanetsDataRef.current%20%3D%20finalPlanets%3B%0AsetPlanetsData(finalPlanets)%3B%0A%7D%0A%7D%0AanimationRef.current%20%3D%20requestAnimationFrame(animate)%3B%0A%7D%3B">
                <div class="codeblock-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-surface border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700">
                    <span class="codeblock-language text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide text-foreground opacity-70 inline">typescript</span>
                    <button class="codeblock-copy-btn inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 text-xs font-medium border rounded transition-all duration-200 bg-background hover:bg-surface text-foreground hover:text-primary border-gray-300 dark:border-gray-600 hover:scale-105 active:scale-95" title="Copy code">
                        <svg class="copy-icon w-4 h-4" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path d="M8 3a1 1 0 011-1h2a1 1 0 110 2H9a1 1 0 01-1-1z" />
                            <path d="M6 3a2 2 0 00-2 2v11a2 2 0 002 2h8a2 2 0 002-2V5a2 2 0 00-2-2 3 3 0 01-3 3H9a3 3 0 01-3-3z" />
                        </svg>
                        <svg class="copied-icon w-4 h-4 hidden" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.707 5.293a1 1 0 010 1.414l-8 8a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 011.414-1.414L8 12.586l7.293-7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        <span class="copy-text inline">Copy</span>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <pre class="codeblock-content p-4 overflow-x-auto font-mono text-sm leading-relaxed bg-surface text-foreground"><code class="language-typescript"><span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_ inline">animate</span> = (<span class="hljs-params inline"><span class="hljs-attr inline">currentTime</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in inline">number</span></span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-keyword inline">if</span> (!lastTimeRef.<span class="hljs-property inline">current</span>) lastTimeRef.<span class="hljs-property inline">current</span> = currentTime;
    <span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> deltaTime = currentTime - lastTimeRef.<span class="hljs-property inline">current</span>;
    lastTimeRef.<span class="hljs-property inline">current</span> = currentTime;
    
    frameCountRef.<span class="hljs-property inline">current</span>++;
    
    <span class="hljs-comment inline">// Frame rate control strategy - update position every 2 frames</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword inline">if</span> (frameCountRef.<span class="hljs-property inline">current</span> % <span class="hljs-number inline">2</span> === <span class="hljs-number inline">0</span>) {
        <span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> currentData = planetsDataRef.<span class="hljs-property inline">current</span>;
        
        <span class="hljs-comment inline">// Update planet positions and angles</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> updatedPlanets = currentData.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">map</span>(<span class="hljs-function inline"><span class="hljs-params inline">planet</span> =&gt;</span> {
            <span class="hljs-keyword inline">if</span> (planet.<span class="hljs-property inline">isPaused</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword inline">return</span> planet;

            <span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> baseSpeed = <span class="hljs-number inline">0.15</span> + planet.<span class="hljs-property inline">orbitIndex</span> * <span class="hljs-number inline">0.08</span>;
            <span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> currentSpeed = baseSpeed * planet.<span class="hljs-property inline">speedMultiplier</span> * planet.<span class="hljs-property inline">collisionSpeedBoost</span>;
            <span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> newAngle = (planet.<span class="hljs-property inline">angle</span> + currentSpeed * deltaTime * <span class="hljs-number inline">0.01</span>) % <span class="hljs-number inline">360</span>;
            <span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> normalizedAngle = newAngle &lt; <span class="hljs-number inline">0</span> ? newAngle + <span class="hljs-number inline">360</span> : newAngle;

            <span class="hljs-keyword inline">return</span> {
                ...planet,
                <span class="hljs-attr inline">angle</span>: normalizedAngle,
                <span class="hljs-attr inline">x</span>: galaxyCenter.<span class="hljs-property inline">x</span> + <span class="hljs-title class_ inline">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">cos</span>(normalizedAngle * <span class="hljs-title class_ inline">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-property inline">PI</span> / <span class="hljs-number inline">180</span>) * planet.<span class="hljs-property inline">orbitRadius</span>,
                <span class="hljs-attr inline">y</span>: galaxyCenter.<span class="hljs-property inline">y</span> + <span class="hljs-title class_ inline">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">sin</span>(normalizedAngle * <span class="hljs-title class_ inline">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-property inline">PI</span> / <span class="hljs-number inline">180</span>) * planet.<span class="hljs-property inline">orbitRadius</span>,
            };
        });

        <span class="hljs-comment inline">// Collision detection every 4 frames (maintain high frequency during stirring)</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword inline">let</span> finalPlanets = updatedPlanets;
        <span class="hljs-keyword inline">if</span> (frameCountRef.<span class="hljs-property inline">current</span> % <span class="hljs-number inline">4</span> === <span class="hljs-number inline">0</span> || isStirring) {
            finalPlanets = <span class="hljs-title function_ inline">detectCollisions</span>(updatedPlanets);
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment inline">// Only update state when there are actual changes</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword inline">if</span> (finalPlanets !== currentData) {
            planetsDataRef.<span class="hljs-property inline">current</span> = finalPlanets;
            <span class="hljs-title function_ inline">setPlanetsData</span>(finalPlanets);
        }
    }
    
    animationRef.<span class="hljs-property inline">current</span> = <span class="hljs-title function_ inline">requestAnimationFrame</span>(animate);
};
</code></pre>
            </div>
        
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">Main functionality explanation:</p>
<ol class="list-decimal list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Initialize timestamp</strong>: Set baseline time on first call</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Calculate time difference</strong>: <code>deltaTime</code> is the milliseconds since the last update</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Update timestamp</strong>: Prepare for next calculation</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Angle accumulation</strong>: Update angle proportionally based on time difference</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="the-001-coefficient-controlling-initial-planet-orbital-speed" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#the-001-coefficient-controlling-initial-planet-orbital-speed" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to The 0.01 coefficient controlling initial planet orbital speed">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            The 0.01 coefficient controlling initial planet orbital speed
        </h3>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">You might have noticed the <code>deltaTime * 0.01</code> coefficient. Its meaning:</p>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>deltaTime</code> is in milliseconds, usually around 16-17ms (60fps)</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed">After multiplying by 0.01, it increases about 0.16-0.17 degrees per frame</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed">This speed makes planet movement look neither too fast to be dizzying nor too slow to be sluggish</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="animation-lifecycle-management" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#animation-lifecycle-management" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Animation Lifecycle Management">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Animation Lifecycle Management
        </h3>

            <div class="enhanced-codeblock relative mb-6 rounded-lg border bg-background border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden shadow-sm" data-enhanced-codeblock="true" data-language="typescript" data-code="useEffect(()%20%3D%3E%20%7B%0AanimationRef.current%20%3D%20requestAnimationFrame(animate)%3B%0Areturn%20()%20%3D%3E%20%7B%0Aif%20(animationRef.current)%20%7B%0AcancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current)%3B%0A%7D%0A%7D%3B%0A%7D%2C%20%5BisPaused%2C%20currentSpeed%5D)%3B">
                <div class="codeblock-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-surface border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700">
                    <span class="codeblock-language text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide text-foreground opacity-70 inline">typescript</span>
                    <button class="codeblock-copy-btn inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 text-xs font-medium border rounded transition-all duration-200 bg-background hover:bg-surface text-foreground hover:text-primary border-gray-300 dark:border-gray-600 hover:scale-105 active:scale-95" title="Copy code">
                        <svg class="copy-icon w-4 h-4" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path d="M8 3a1 1 0 011-1h2a1 1 0 110 2H9a1 1 0 01-1-1z" />
                            <path d="M6 3a2 2 0 00-2 2v11a2 2 0 002 2h8a2 2 0 002-2V5a2 2 0 00-2-2 3 3 0 01-3 3H9a3 3 0 01-3-3z" />
                        </svg>
                        <svg class="copied-icon w-4 h-4 hidden" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.707 5.293a1 1 0 010 1.414l-8 8a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 011.414-1.414L8 12.586l7.293-7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        <span class="copy-text inline">Copy</span>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <pre class="codeblock-content p-4 overflow-x-auto font-mono text-sm leading-relaxed bg-surface text-foreground"><code class="language-typescript"><span class="hljs-title function_ inline">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function inline">() =&gt;</span> {
    animationRef.<span class="hljs-property inline">current</span> = <span class="hljs-title function_ inline">requestAnimationFrame</span>(animate);
    
    <span class="hljs-keyword inline">return</span> <span class="hljs-function inline">() =&gt;</span> {
        <span class="hljs-keyword inline">if</span> (animationRef.<span class="hljs-property inline">current</span>) {
            <span class="hljs-title function_ inline">cancelAnimationFrame</span>(animationRef.<span class="hljs-property inline">current</span>);
        }
    };
}, [isPaused, currentSpeed]);
</code></pre>
            </div>
        
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">This effect ensures:</p>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed">Start animation when component mounts</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed">Clean up animation when component unmounts, preventing memory leaks</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed">Restart animation loop when pause state or speed changes</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="simulating-celestial-body-orbital-speed-differences" class="group relative text-3xl font-semibold mt-6 mb-3 text-foreground leading-tight">
            <a href="#simulating-celestial-body-orbital-speed-differences" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Simulating Celestial Body Orbital Speed Differences">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Simulating Celestial Body Orbital Speed Differences
        </h2>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">In the real solar system, inner planets orbit faster than outer planets. This physical phenomenon is known as Kepler’s Third Law, and I’ve simulated this effect in the galaxy:</p>

            <div class="enhanced-codeblock relative mb-6 rounded-lg border bg-background border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden shadow-sm" data-enhanced-codeblock="true" data-language="typescript" data-code="const%20baseSpeed%20%3D%200.15%20%2B%20orbitIndex%20*%200.08%3B%20%2F%2F%20Base%20speed%20plus%20orbital%20coefficient%0Aconst%20currentSpeed%20%3D%20baseSpeed%20*%20speedMultiplier%20*%20collisionSpeedBoost%3B">
                <div class="codeblock-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-surface border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700">
                    <span class="codeblock-language text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide text-foreground opacity-70 inline">typescript</span>
                    <button class="codeblock-copy-btn inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 text-xs font-medium border rounded transition-all duration-200 bg-background hover:bg-surface text-foreground hover:text-primary border-gray-300 dark:border-gray-600 hover:scale-105 active:scale-95" title="Copy code">
                        <svg class="copy-icon w-4 h-4" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path d="M8 3a1 1 0 011-1h2a1 1 0 110 2H9a1 1 0 01-1-1z" />
                            <path d="M6 3a2 2 0 00-2 2v11a2 2 0 002 2h8a2 2 0 002-2V5a2 2 0 00-2-2 3 3 0 01-3 3H9a3 3 0 01-3-3z" />
                        </svg>
                        <svg class="copied-icon w-4 h-4 hidden" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.707 5.293a1 1 0 010 1.414l-8 8a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 011.414-1.414L8 12.586l7.293-7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        <span class="copy-text inline">Copy</span>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <pre class="codeblock-content p-4 overflow-x-auto font-mono text-sm leading-relaxed bg-surface text-foreground"><code class="language-typescript"><span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> baseSpeed = <span class="hljs-number inline">0.15</span> + orbitIndex * <span class="hljs-number inline">0.08</span>; <span class="hljs-comment inline">// Base speed plus orbital coefficient</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> currentSpeed = baseSpeed * speedMultiplier * collisionSpeedBoost;
</code></pre>
            </div>
        
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">Let’s look at the actual speed distribution:</p>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed">1st orbit (orbitIndex=0): 0.15 - fastest</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed">2nd orbit (orbitIndex=1): 0.23</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed">3rd orbit (orbitIndex=2): 0.31</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed">4th orbit (orbitIndex=3): 0.39</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed">5th orbit (orbitIndex=4): 0.47</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed">6th orbit (orbitIndex=5): 0.55</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed">7th orbit (orbitIndex=6): 0.63 - slowest</li>
</ul>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">…But! If you observe closely, you’ll notice that in my Skills Galaxy, outer orbits actually rotate faster than inner orbits (higher numerical values). This is opposite to the real physical world.</p>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">I chose to deliberately keep this “bug” because from the actual visual experience perspective, having outer orbits rotate slightly faster actually creates better dynamic feeling. This is artistic effect &gt; physical accuracy.</p>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground"><code>speedMultiplier</code> is an extended property of the planet component that reserves an interface for the “stir galaxy” function, normally staying at 1, and can become 4-14 times faster when acceleration is needed.</p>
<h2 id="interaction-feedback" class="group relative text-3xl font-semibold mt-6 mb-3 text-foreground leading-tight">
            <a href="#interaction-feedback" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Interaction Feedback">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">

<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">Event handlers optimized with <code>useCallback</code> ensure callback function reference stability. When users hover, the corresponding planet gracefully stops while updating the hover state, as if time has been frozen. This detail allows users to carefully examine planet information without being distracted by continuous motion.</p>

<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">This multi-layer conditional style system allows planets to display rich visual feedback based on different states:</p>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Default state</strong>: Semi-transparent white, low-key and elegant</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Hover state</strong>: Theme color highlight with increased shadow</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Stirring state</strong>: Purple emphasis, indicating high-speed operation</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Collision state</strong>: Red warning, marking dangerous state</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Burst state</strong>: Yellow highlight, showing energy release</li>

<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">The “stir galaxy” function simulates the effect of applying external force to the galaxy, making this galaxy appear less rigid.</p>

                        </svg>
                        <span class="copy-text inline">Copy</span>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <pre class="codeblock-content p-4 overflow-x-auto font-mono text-sm leading-relaxed bg-surface text-foreground"><code class="language-typescript"><span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> numPlanetsToStir = <span class="hljs-title class_ inline">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">min</span>(resumeData.<span class="hljs-property inline">skills</span>.<span class="hljs-property inline">length</span>, 
    <span class="hljs-title class_ inline">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">floor</span>(resumeData.<span class="hljs-property inline">skills</span>.<span class="hljs-property inline">length</span> * <span class="hljs-title class_ inline">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">random</span>() + <span class="hljs-number inline">1</span>));
</code></pre>
            </div>
        
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>resumeData.skills.length * Math.random() + 1</code>: Generates a random number between 1 and the total count</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>Math.floor()</code>: Rounds down to integer</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><code>Math.min()</code>: Ensures it doesn’t exceed the total number of planets</li>
</ul>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">This means each time we stir, a random number of planets will be affected, adding unpredictability.</p>
<h3 id="avoiding-duplicate-selection" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#avoiding-duplicate-selection" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Avoiding Duplicate Selection">

                </svg>
            </a>
            Avoiding Duplicate Selection
        </h3>

                <pre class="codeblock-content p-4 overflow-x-auto font-mono text-sm leading-relaxed bg-surface text-foreground"><code class="language-typescript"><span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> <span class="hljs-attr inline">indicesToStir</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in inline">number</span>[] = [];

<span class="hljs-keyword inline">while</span> (indicesToStir.<span class="hljs-property inline">length</span> &lt; numPlanetsToStir) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword inline">const</span> randomIndex = <span class="hljs-title class_ inline">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">floor</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_ inline">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">random</span>() * resumeData.<span class="hljs-property inline">skills</span>.<span class="hljs-property inline">length</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword inline">if</span> (!indicesToStir.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">includes</span>(randomIndex)) {
        indicesToStir.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">push</span>(randomIndex);
    }
}
</code></pre>
            </div>
        
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">This while loop ensures each planet is selected at most once, avoiding wasted “stirring quota” situations.</p>

<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">This animation creates a “breathing” effect:</p>
<ul class="list-disc list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">30px shadow</strong>: Contracted state, more restrained</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">50px shadow</strong>: Expanded state, radiating light</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">0.5→0.8→0.5 opacity</strong>: Combined with size changes, enhances light-dark contrast</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">3-second cycle</strong>: Not too fast to appear restless, not too slow to seem sluggish</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">easeInOut</strong>: Natural acceleration and deceleration, like real breathing</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="multi-layer-glow" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#multi-layer-glow" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Multi-layer Glow">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">

                </svg>
            </a>
            Multi-layer Glow
        </h3>

            <div class="enhanced-codeblock relative mb-6 rounded-lg border bg-background border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden shadow-sm" data-enhanced-codeblock="true" data-language="typescript" data-code="%7B%2F*%20Main%20sun%20body%20*%2F%7D%0A%22w-full%20h-full%20rounded-full%20bg-gradient-to-br%20from-amber-300%20via-yellow-400%20to-orange-500%22%3E%0A%F0%9F%91%A8%E2%80%8D%F0%9F%92%BB%0A%7B%2F*%20Background%20glow%20*%2F%7D%0A%22absolute%20inset-0%20rounded-full%20bg-gradient-to-br%20from-amber-300%2F30%20to-orange-500%2F30%20animate-pulse%20-z-10%20scale-150%22%2F%3E">

    👨‍💻

</code></pre>
            </div>
        
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">There are two layers of light effects:</p>
<ol class="list-decimal list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Main sun body</strong>: Solid gradient colors from amber to orange</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Background glow</strong>: Larger, more transparent, pulsating light ring</li>
</ol>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground"><code>scale-150</code> makes the background glow 50% larger than the main body, <code>-z-10</code> ensures it stays in the background, creating multi-layered light effects.</p>
<h2 id="dynamic-layout-central-positioning-system" class="group relative text-3xl font-semibold mt-6 mb-3 text-foreground leading-tight">
            <a href="#dynamic-layout-central-positioning-system" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Dynamic Layout Central Positioning System">
                <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12.586 4.586a2 2 0 112.828 2.828l-3 3a2 2 0 01-2.828 0 1 1 0 11.414-1.414 4 4 0 105.656 0l3-3a4 4 0 00-5.656-5.656l-1.5 1.5a1 1 0 101.414 1.414l1.5-1.5zm-5 5a2 2 0 012.828 0 1 1 0 101.414-1.414 4 4 0 10-5.656 0l-3 3a4 4 0 105.656 5.656l1.5-1.5a1 1 0 10-1.414-1.414l-1.5 1.5a2 2 0 11-2.828-2.828l3-3z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
            </a>
            Dynamic Layout Central Positioning System
        </h2>
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">In responsive design, the galaxy’s center position needs to adjust dynamically based on container size, preventing galaxy displacement when window size changes.</p>
<h3 id="center-calculation" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">

                </svg>
            </a>
            Center Calculation
        </h3>

            <div class="enhanced-codeblock relative mb-6 rounded-lg border bg-background border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden shadow-sm" data-enhanced-codeblock="true" data-language="typescript" data-code="const%20updateCenter%20%3D%20()%20%3D%3E%20%7B%0Aif%20(galaxyRef.current)%20%7B%0Aconst%20rect%20%3D%20galaxyRef.current.getBoundingClientRect()%3B%0AsetGalaxyCenter(%7B%0Ax%3A%20rect.width%20%2F%202%2C%0Ay%3A%20rect.height%20%2F%202%0A%7D)%3B%0A%7D%0A%7D%3B">

<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground"><code>getBoundingClientRect()</code> is the most reliable method to get DOM element actual dimensions, returning the element’s actual rendered size in the page, including padding and all style effects.</p>
<h3 id="responsive-listening" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#responsive-listening" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Responsive Listening">

            </a>
            Responsive Listening
        </h3>

            <div class="enhanced-codeblock relative mb-6 rounded-lg border bg-background border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden shadow-sm" data-enhanced-codeblock="true" data-language="typescript" data-code="useEffect(()%20%3D%3E%20%7B%0AupdateCenter()%3B%0Awindow.addEventListener('resize'%2C%20updateCenter)%3B%0Areturn%20()%20%3D%3E%20window.removeEventListener('resize'%2C%20updateCenter)%3B%0A%7D%2C%20%5B%5D)%3B">

    <span class="hljs-title function_ inline">updateCenter</span>();
    <span class="hljs-variable language_ inline">window</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">addEventListener</span>(<span class="hljs-string inline">&#x27;resize&#x27;</span>, updateCenter);
    
    <span class="hljs-keyword inline">return</span> <span class="hljs-function inline">() =&gt;</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_ inline">window</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_ inline">removeEventListener</span>(<span class="hljs-string inline">&#x27;resize&#x27;</span>, updateCenter);
}, []);
</code></pre>
            </div>
        
<p class="text-base leading-7 mb-4 text-foreground">This effect does three things:</p>
<ol class="list-decimal list-inside mb-4 pl-6 space-y-2">
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Component mount</strong>: Immediately calculate center position once</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Window resize</strong>: Recalculate center position</li>
<li class="text-foreground leading-relaxed"><strong class="font-bold text-foreground">Component unmount</strong>: Clean up event listeners to prevent memory leaks</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="default-value-safety-strategy" class="group relative text-2xl font-semibold mt-5 mb-2 text-foreground leading-snug">
            <a href="#default-value-safety-strategy" class="absolute -left-6 top-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity text-primary/60 hover:text-primary" aria-label="Link to Default Value Safety Strategy">

                </svg>
            </a>
            Default Value Safety Strategy
        </h3>

            <div class="enhanced-codeblock relative mb-6 rounded-lg border bg-background border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden shadow-sm" data-enhanced-codeblock="true" data-language="typescript" data-code="const%20%5BgalaxyCenter%2C%20setGalaxyCenter%5D%20%3D%20useState(%7Bx%3A%20350%2C%20y%3A%20350%7D)%3B">
